\begin{itemize}

  Atama operatÃ¶rÃ¼ olarak ``kÃ¼Ã§Ã¼ktÃ¼r'' simgesi ile ``kÄ±sa Ã§izgi'' simgesi \textbf{\texttt{\textless{}-}} simgeleri kullanÄ±labilir.
\item

\item
  Ancak \textbf{\texttt{=}} operatÃ¶rÃ¼ programlama yaparken matematiksel eÅŸitlikle karÄ±ÅŸabilmektedir.
\item
  Atama yapÄ±lacak nesne isimlendirilirken harflerle (A* Z veya a* z) baÅŸlamalÄ±dÄ±r.
\item
  Ä°simlendirmeye harfle baÅŸlandÄ±ktan sonra rakamlar (0* 9), nokta (.) ve alt cizgi (\_) ile devam edilebilmektedir.
\item
  R harflerin kÃ¼Ã§Ã¼k ve ya bÃ¼yÃ¼k olmasÄ±na karÅŸÄ± duyarlÄ±dÄ±r.
\item

  AyrÄ±ca \textbf{c,C,D,F,I,q,t,T} gibi tek harfli nesne ismi kullanmaktan kaÃ§Ä±nÄ±lmalÄ±dÄ±r; bunlarÄ±n R'da Ã¶zel anlamlarÄ± bulunmaktadÄ±r.

  R yazÄ±lÄ±mÄ±nda \textbf{\#} iÅŸareti ile baÅŸlayan satÄ±r, yorum satÄ±rÄ±dÄ±r.
\item
  Genellikle komutlarÄ±n anlamÄ±nÄ± aÃ§Ä±klamak iÃ§in kullanÄ±lmaktadÄ±r.
\item
  R, bu satÄ±rlarÄ± dikkate almaz, bunlar sadece kullanÄ±cÄ±lar iÃ§in bilgi ve hatÄ±rlatÄ±cÄ± aÃ§Ä±klamalarÄ± iÃ§ermektedir.

\item

  Bir fonksiyonun aldÄ±ÄŸÄ± tÃ¼m argÃ¼manlara yardÄ±m dokÃ¼mantasyonunu kullanarak \texttt{?function} formatÄ±nÄ± kullanarak bakabilirsiniz. \begin{info}
EÄŸer internette kod Ã¶rneklerine bakÄ±yorsanÄ±z, sÄ±k sÄ±k
\texttt{set.seed()} fonksiyonu ile baÅŸlayan kodlar gÃ¶rebilirsiniz. Bu

saÄŸlayacaktÄ±r (bazÄ± durumlarda yapmak istediÄŸiniz ÅŸey bu olmayabilir).
Bu Ã¶rnekte \texttt{set.seed()} diyoruz, bu aynÄ± rastgele sayÄ±larÄ±
alacaÄŸÄ±nÄ±z anlamÄ±na geliyor.
\end{info}

\hypertarget{arguxfcman-isimleri}{%

\begin{itemize}

  Ã–nemli olarak, eÄŸer argÃ¼man isimlerini yazmazsanÄ±z, R argÃ¼manlarÄ±n varsayÄ±lan sÄ±rasÄ±nÄ± kullanacaktÄ±r, yani \texttt{rnorm} iÃ§in girdiÄŸiniz ilk sayÄ±nÄ±n \texttt{n} olduÄŸunu varsayacaktÄ±r. ikinci sayÄ± \texttt{mean} ve Ã¼Ã§Ã¼ncÃ¼ sayÄ± \texttt{sd}dir.

  \item
    OrtalamasÄ± 6 ve SD'si 50 olan 10 sayÄ±dan oluÅŸan bir veri seti\\
  \end{enumerate}

  \begin{enumerate}
  \def\labelenumi{(\Alph{enumi})}
  \setcounter{enumi}{1}
  \tightlist
  \item
    OrtalamasÄ± 50 ve SD'si 10 olan 6 sayÄ±dan oluÅŸan bir veri seti\\

    OrtalamasÄ± 10 ve SD'si 6 olan 50 sayÄ±dan oluÅŸan bir veri seti
  \end{enumerate}
\end{itemize}

AÃ§Ä±klama

\texttt{rnorm()} iÃ§in varsayÄ±lan biÃ§im \texttt{rnorm(n,\ mean,\ sd)} ÅŸeklindedir. Bir fonksiyonun her bir argÃ¼manÄ±nÄ±n ne iÅŸe yaradÄ±ÄŸÄ±nÄ± hatÄ±rlamak iÃ§in yardÄ±ma ihtiyacÄ±nÄ±z varsa, \texttt{?rnorm} komutunu Ã§alÄ±ÅŸtÄ±rarak yardÄ±m belgelerine bakÄ±n

\textbf{Soru 3.} AynÄ± isimde fonksiyonlara sahip iki paketiniz varsa ve tam olarak hangi paketin kullanÄ±lacaÄŸÄ±nÄ± belirtmek istiyorsanÄ±z, hangi kodu kullanÄ±rsÄ±nÄ±z?

\textbf{BÃ¼yÃ¼k KÃ¼Ã§Ã¼k Harf DÃ¼zenleme FonksiyonlarÄ±} \texttt{toupper()} ve \texttt{tolower()}

\hypertarget{seq}{%
\subsection{seq()}\label{seq}}

\begin{itemize}
\item

\begin{itemize}

\item

\begin{try}

\begin{itemize}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{n }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{nrow}\NormalTok{(iris) }\CommentTok{\# toplam satÄ±r sayÄ±sÄ±}

\NormalTok{simule\_deger }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \FunctionTok{rnorm}\NormalTok{(n, mu, sd)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{itemize}
\item
  Bir kod parÃ§asÄ±nÄ±, Ã¶zellikle kod rapor metninde aÃ§Ä±klanmamÄ±ÅŸsa, orada ne yaptÄ±ÄŸÄ±nÄ±zÄ± aÃ§Ä±klayan bir yorumla baÅŸlatmak genellikle iyi bir uygulamadÄ±r.
\item
  Nesnelerinizi aÃ§Ä±k bir ÅŸekilde adlandÄ±rÄ±rsanÄ±z, genellikle aÃ§Ä±klayÄ±cÄ± yorumlar eklemeniz gerekmez. Ã–rneÄŸin, yukarÄ±daki Ã¼Ã§ nesneyi n\_iris, ort\_petal ve sd\_petal olarak adlandÄ±rmÄ±ÅŸ olsaydÄ±m, yorumlarÄ± atlardÄ±m.
\item
  YorumlarÄ±n bir baÅŸka kullanÄ±mÄ± da Ã§alÄ±ÅŸtÄ±rmak istemediÄŸiniz ancak silmek de istemediÄŸiniz bir kod bÃ¶lÃ¼mÃ¼nÃ¼ ``yorumlamaktÄ±r''. Ã–rneÄŸin, bir paketi yÃ¼klemek iÃ§in kullanÄ±lan kodu kodunuza dahil edebilirsiniz, ancak kodun her Ã§alÄ±ÅŸtÄ±rÄ±ldÄ±ÄŸÄ±nda uzun bir yÃ¼klemeye zorlamamasÄ± iÃ§in her zaman yorumlamanÄ±z gerekir.
\end{itemize}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# install.packages("dplyr")}
\CommentTok{\# install.packages("tidyr")}
\CommentTok{\# install.packages("ggplot2")}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{info}
SatÄ±rlarÄ± seÃ§ip Cmd-shift-C (Mac) veya Ctrl-shift-C (Windows) yazarak aynÄ± anda birden fazla satÄ±ra yorum yazabilir veya yorumu kaldÄ±rabilirsiniz.

\end{info}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  Kodunuzu iyi bir ÅŸekilde yorumlamak biraz sanattÄ±r. Bu beceriyi geliÅŸtirmenin en iyi yolu, baÅŸkalarÄ±nÄ±n kodlarÄ±nÄ± okumak ve baÅŸkalarÄ±nÄ±n kodunuzu incelemesini saÄŸlamaktÄ±r.
\end{itemize}

\item

\begin{warning}

Bu format varsayÄ±lan olarak numaralandÄ±rÄ±lmÄ±ÅŸ bÃ¶lÃ¼mler bulunuyor, numaralandÄ±rma bunu istemiyorsanÄ±z \texttt{YAML} bÃ¶lÃ¼mÃ¼nde \texttt{number\_sections:\ false} ayarÄ±nÄ± yapÄ±n. NumaralandÄ±rÄ±lmÄ±ÅŸ bÃ¶lÃ¼mleri kaldÄ±rÄ±rsanÄ±z, \texttt{\textbackslash{}@ref(sonuclar)} gibi baÄŸlantÄ±lar ``??'' gÃ¶sterecektir, bu nedenle bunun yerine aÅŸaÄŸÄ±daki gibi URL baÄŸlantÄ± sÃ¶zdizimini kullanmanÄ±z gerekir:

\begin{verbatim}
Son aÃ§Ä±klamalar iÃ§in [son bÃ¶lÃ¼me](#sonuclar) bakÄ±nÄ±z.
\end{verbatim}

\hypertarget{kaynakuxe7a}{%
\section{KaynakÃ§a}\label{kaynakuxe7a}}

R Markdown'da metin iÃ§i referanslar yapmanÄ±n ve otomatik olarak bir kaynakÃ§a oluÅŸturmanÄ±n birkaÃ§ yolu vardÄ±r. Markdown dosyalarÄ±nÄ±n, atÄ±fta bulunmanÄ±z gereken referanslarÄ± iÃ§eren bir BibTex veya JSON dosyasÄ±na (referanslarÄ± belirli bir formatta iÃ§eren dÃ¼z bir metin dosyasÄ±) baÄŸlanmasÄ± gerekir. Bu dosyanÄ±n adÄ±nÄ± bibliography: refs.bib gibi YAML baÅŸlÄ±ÄŸÄ±nda belirtirsiniz ve \citep{tidyverse} gibi bir @ sembolÃ¼ ve kÄ±sa ad kullanarak metin iÃ§inde referanslara atÄ±fta bulunursunuz. ReferanslarÄ±nÄ±zÄ± Ã¶rneÄŸin APA stilinde biÃ§imlendirmek iÃ§in bir Citation Style Language (.csl) dosyasÄ± da ekleyebilirsiniz.

a \href{https://bookdown.org/yihui/rmarkdown-cookbook/bibliography.html}{bibliography}

\begin{verbatim}
---
title: "My Paper"
author: "Me"
output: 
  html_document:
    toc: true
bibliography: refs.bib
csl: apa.csl
\end{verbatim}

\hypertarget{referans-yazux131lux131mdan-duxf6nuxfcux15ftuxfcrme}{%
\subsection{Referans yazÄ±lÄ±mdan dÃ¶nÃ¼ÅŸtÃ¼rme}\label{referans-yazux131lux131mdan-duxf6nuxfcux15ftuxfcrme}}

EndNote veya Zotero gibi Ã§oÄŸu referans yazÄ±lÄ±mÄ± BibTeX formatÄ±na aktarabilen dÄ±ÅŸa aktarma seÃ§eneklerine sahiptir. Ortaya Ã§Ä±kan dosyadaki kÄ±sa adlarÄ± kontrol etmeniz yeterlidir.

\begin{warning}
Bir referans programÄ± kullanmak hayatÄ±nÄ±zÄ± Ã§ok daha kolaylaÅŸtÄ±racaktÄ±r. Zotero muhtemelen en iyisidir.

\end{warning}

DÄ±ÅŸa aktarÄ±lan dosya ÅŸu ÅŸekilde gÃ¶rÃ¼nmelidir:

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]

We suggest eight open science practices that novice graduate students could begin adopting today. The topics we cover include journal clubs, project workflow, preprints, reproducible code, data sharing, transparent writing, preregistration, and registered reports. To address concerns about not knowing how to engage in open science practices, we provide a difficulty rating of each behavior (easy, medium, difficult), present them in order of suggested adoption, and follow the format of what, why, how, and worries. We give graduate students ideas on how to approach conversations with their advisors/collaborators, ideas on how to integrate open science practices within the graduate school framework, and specific resources on how to engage with each behavior. We emphasize that engaging in open science behaviors need not be an all or nothing approach, but rather graduate students can engage with any number of the behaviors outlined.\},}

\hypertarget{bibtex-dosyasux131-oluux15fturma}{%
\subsection{BibTeX DosyasÄ± OluÅŸturma}\label{bibtex-dosyasux131-oluux15fturma}}

ReferanslarÄ± manuel olarak da ekleyebilirsiniz. RStudio'da \textbf{\texttt{File}} \textgreater{} \textbf{\texttt{New\ File...}} \textgreater{} \textbf{\texttt{Text\ File}} seÃ§eneÄŸine gidin. \textgreater{} Metin DosyasÄ±'na gidin ve dosyayÄ± ``refs.bib'' olarak kaydedin.

ArdÄ±ndan, YAML baÅŸlÄ±ÄŸÄ±nÄ±za \texttt{bibliography:\ refs.bib} satÄ±rÄ±nÄ± ekleyin.

\hypertarget{referans-ekleme}{%
\subsection{Referans ekleme}\label{referans-ekleme}}

Bir dergi makalesine aÅŸaÄŸÄ±daki formatta referanslar ekleyebilirsiniz:

\begin{verbatim}
@article{shortname,
  author = {Author One and Author Two and Author Three},
  title = {Paper Title},
  journal = {Journal Title},
  volume = {vol},
  number = {issue},
  pages = {startpage--endpage},
  year = {year},
  doi = {doi}
}
\end{verbatim}

Kitaplara, teknik raporlara ve daha fazlasÄ±na atÄ±fta bulunma talimatlarÄ± iÃ§in BibTeX formatÄ±na iliÅŸkin eksiksiz bir kÄ±lavuza bakÄ±n.

citation() ve toBibtex() fonksiyonlarÄ±nÄ± kullanarak bir R paketi iÃ§in referans alabilirsiniz. Bibtex giriÅŸini bibliography.bib dosyanÄ±za yapÄ±ÅŸtÄ±rabilirsiniz. Referansa atÄ±fta bulunmak iÃ§in ilk virgÃ¼lden Ã¶nce kÄ±sa bir ad (Ã¶rneÄŸin, ``ggplot2'') eklediÄŸinizden emin olun.

See \href{https://www.bibtex.com/g/bibtex-format/}{A complete guide to the BibTeX format} kitaplara, teknik raporlara ve daha fazlasÄ±na atÄ±fta bulunma talimatlarÄ± iÃ§in.

Bir R paketinin referansÄ±nÄ± \texttt{citation()} ve \texttt{toBibtex()} fonksiyonlarÄ±nÄ± kullanarak alabilirsiniz. Bibtex giriÅŸini bibliography.bib dosyanÄ±za yapÄ±ÅŸtÄ±rabilirsiniz. Referansa atÄ±fta bulunmak iÃ§in ilk virgÃ¼lden Ã¶nce kÄ±sa bir ad (Ã¶rneÄŸin, ``ggplot2'') eklediÄŸinizden emin olun.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\FunctionTok{citation}\NormalTok{(}\AttributeTok{package=}\StringTok{"ggplot2"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%} \FunctionTok{toBibtex}\NormalTok{()}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## @Book{,
##   author = {Hadley Wickham},
##   title = {ggplot2: Elegant Graphics for Data Analysis},
##   publisher = {Springer-Verlag New York},
##   year = {2016},
##   isbn = {978-3-319-24277-4},
##   url = {https://ggplot2.tidyverse.org},
## }
\end{verbatim}

\href{https://scholar.google.com/}{Google Scholar} giriÅŸlerinde BibTeX atÄ±f seÃ§eneÄŸi vardÄ±r. DOI'yi kendiniz eklemeniz gerekse de, Zotero tarayÄ±cÄ± baÄŸlayÄ±cÄ±sÄ± aracÄ±lÄ±ÄŸÄ±yla bir atÄ±f ekleyemiyorsanÄ±z, ilgili deÄŸerleri almanÄ±n en kolay yolu genellikle budur. Ã–nerilen kÄ±sa adÄ± koruyabilir veya sizin iÃ§in daha anlamlÄ± olan bir adla deÄŸiÅŸtirebilirsiniz.

\hypertarget{referanslara-atux131fta-bulunma}{%
\subsection{Referanslara atÄ±fta bulunma}\label{referanslara-atux131fta-bulunma}}

Metin iÃ§inde referanslarÄ± bu ÅŸekilde gÃ¶sterebilirsiniz:

\begin{verbatim}
This tutorial uses several R packages [@tidyverse;@rmarkdown].
\end{verbatim}

Bu eÄŸitimde Ã§eÅŸitli R paketleri kullanÄ±lmaktadÄ±r (Allaire vd., 2018; Wickham, 2017).

Sadece yÄ±lÄ± istiyorsanÄ±z @'nin Ã¶nÃ¼ne bir eksi koyun:

\hypertarget{atux131f-yapux131lmayan-referanslar}{%
\subsection{AtÄ±f yapÄ±lmayan referanslar}\label{atux131f-yapux131lmayan-referanslar}}

Bir Ã¶ÄŸeyi kaynak gÃ¶stermeden referans bÃ¶lÃ¼mÃ¼ne eklemek istiyorsanÄ±z, bunu YAML baÅŸlÄ±ÄŸÄ±na ÅŸu ÅŸekilde ekleyin:

\begin{verbatim}

  @kathawalla_easing_2021, @broman2018data, @nordmann2022data
\end{verbatim}

Ya da .bib dosyasÄ±ndaki tÃ¼m Ã¶ÄŸeleri ÅŸu ÅŸekilde ekleyin:

\begin{verbatim}

\end{verbatim}

\hypertarget{atux131f-stilleri}{%
\subsection{AtÄ±f Stilleri}\label{atux131f-stilleri}}

Ã‡eÅŸitli dergiler iÃ§in \href{https://www.zotero.org/styles}{stil dosyalarÄ±nÄ±n} bir listesini arayabilir ve kaynakÃ§anÄ±zÄ± belirli bir derginin stiline gÃ¶re biÃ§imlendirecek bir dosya indirebilirsiniz. YAML baÅŸlÄ±ÄŸÄ±nÄ±za \texttt{csl:\ filename.csl} satÄ±rÄ±nÄ± eklemeniz gerekir.

\begin{try}

\hypertarget{referens-buxf6luxfcmuxfc}{%
\subsection{Referens BÃ¶lÃ¼mÃ¼}\label{referens-buxf6luxfcmuxfc}}

VarsayÄ±lan olarak, referans bÃ¶lÃ¼mÃ¼ belgenin sonuna eklenir. Konumu deÄŸiÅŸtirmek istiyorsanÄ±z (Ã¶rneÄŸin, referanslardan sonra ÅŸekil ve tablo eklemek iÃ§in), referanslarÄ± istediÄŸiniz yere \texttt{\textless{}div\ id="refs"\textgreater{}\textless{}/div\textgreater{}} ekleyin.

\begin{try}

\end{try}

  Ali, Su ve Ece'nin boylarÄ±nÄ±n ve kilolarÄ±nÄ±n seÃ§ilmesi
\end{itemize}

\texttt{attach()} fonksiyonu ile bir veri setinin sÃ¼tunlarÄ± sÃ¼tun isimi ile enviromente eklenir. AynÄ± iÅŸlem \texttt{detach()} fonksiyonu ile tersine alÄ±nabilir.

## [1] ".GlobalEnv" "women"
\end{verbatim}

\hypertarget{kendinizi-test-edin-1}{%
\subsection{Kendinizi Test Edin}\label{kendinizi-test-edin-1}}

\textbf{S1.} SÄ±rayla deÄŸiÅŸken adlarÄ± TamSayi, OndalikSayi, Karakter, MantÄ±ksal, FaktÃ¶r olan 5 deÄŸiÅŸkenli hiÃ§bir gÃ¶zlemi olmayan bir data.frame oluÅŸturmanÄ±zÄ± ve bu data.framenin yapÄ±sÄ±nÄ± yazdÄ±rmanÄ±zÄ± bekliyorum. Beklenen Ã§Ä±ktÄ± aÅŸaÄŸÄ±daki gibi olmalÄ±dÄ±r.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{[}\DecValTok{1}\NormalTok{] }\StringTok{"Bos data.framenin yapÄ±sÄ±:"}
\StringTok{\textquotesingle{}data.frame\textquotesingle{}}\SpecialCharTok{:}   \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{ obs. of  }\DecValTok{5}\NormalTok{ variables}\SpecialCharTok{:}  
 \ErrorTok{$}\NormalTok{ TamSayi    }\SpecialCharTok{:}\NormalTok{ int   }
 \SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{ OndalikSayi}\SpecialCharTok{:}\NormalTok{ num  }
 \SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{ Karakter   }\SpecialCharTok{:}\NormalTok{ chr  }
 \SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{ Mantiksal  }\SpecialCharTok{:}\NormalTok{ logi  }
 \SpecialCharTok{$}\NormalTok{ Faktor     }\SpecialCharTok{:}\NormalTok{ Factor w}\SpecialCharTok{/} \DecValTok{0}\NormalTok{ levels}\SpecialCharTok{:}  
\ConstantTok{NULL}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\textbf{S2.} AÅŸaÄŸÄ±da size verilen dÃ¶rt vektÃ¶rden bir veri seti oluÅŸturunuz. OluÅŸturduÄŸunuz veri setinin deneme sÃ¼tunundaki eksik veri sayÄ±sÄ±nÄ± hesaplayan komut yazÄ±nÄ±z.

\begin{Shaded}

  ğŸ”— \href{https://psyteachr.github.io/data-skills-v1/getting-to-know-the-data.html}{Linkte} yer alan sayfayÄ± inceleyiniz. Bu sayfada bir veri setini incelemeniz ve bu veri seti ile ilgili sorulara cevap vermeniz beklenemketedir.
\item
  ğŸ”—\href{https://psyteachr.github.io/data-skills-v1/loading-data.html}{Linkte} yer alan sayfada sizden iki veri setini okumanÄ±z beklenmeketdir. Bu iki veri setini okuduktan sonra da hazÄ±r kodlarÄ± incelemeniz ve bu kodlar ile ilgili sorulara cevap vermeniz beklenmektedir.
\end{itemize}

\item
  \textbf{\%\textgreater\%} operatorÃ¼ sÄ±k kullanÄ±lan bir operatÃ¶rdÃ¼r.

\begin{Shaded}

\begin{Shaded}

  \FunctionTok{filter}\NormalTok{(country }\SpecialCharTok{==} \StringTok{"Canada"}\NormalTok{) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}

\begin{itemize}
\item
  bizi fazla yazmaktan kurtarÄ±r.
\item
  kodu okunabilir kÄ±lar.
\item
  zincirlemeye/baÄŸlamaya izin verir.
\item
  Veri dÃ¼zenleme iÅŸlerinde her zaman kullanÄ±ÅŸlÄ±dÄ±r.
\item
  pipe, her bir fonksiyonu ayrÄ± bir satÄ±rda bulundurduÄŸunuzda en net ÅŸekilde okunur.
\end{itemize}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{veri }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{ilk\_fonksiyon}\NormalTok{(.....) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{ikinci\_fonksiyon}\NormalTok{(.....) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}
  \FunctionTok{ucuncu\_fonksiyon}\NormalTok{(.....) }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}\NormalTok{ ...}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{itemize}
\item
  pipenin solundaki Ã¶ÄŸeler, saÄŸdaki fonksiyonun ilk argÃ¼manÄ±na iletilir.
\item
  Fonksiyon ilk argÃ¼manÄ± olan veriyi pipenin \textbf{solundan} alÄ±r, kalan argÃ¼manlar fonksiyonun \textbf{saÄŸÄ±ndadÄ±r.}
\item
  BazÄ± fonksiyonlarÄ±n, ilk argÃ¼manÄ± veri seti olmayabilir. Bu durumda veri seti argÃ¼man deÄŸeri \textbf{.} olarak kullanÄ±labilir.

\begin{itemize}

  \textbf{filter()} fonksiyonunu \textbf{mantÄ±ksal operatorler} kullanarak satÄ±r bazÄ±nda seÃ§im yapar.
\item
  \textbf{mantÄ±ksal operatorler} koÅŸullarÄ± test eder.
\end{itemize}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{x }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{1}
\NormalTok{x}\SpecialCharTok{==}\DecValTok{1}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## [1] TRUE
\end{verbatim}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{x }\OtherTok{\textless{}{-}} \DecValTok{1}
\NormalTok{x}\SpecialCharTok{!=}\DecValTok{1}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## [1] FALSE
\end{verbatim}

\begin{itemize}
\item
  TRUE, FALSE ve NA deÄŸerleri alÄ±rlar.
\item
  \textbf{filter()} fonksiyonunu ise koÅŸulun saÄŸlandÄ±ÄŸÄ± satÄ±rlarÄ± seÃ§er.

  \begin{itemize}
  \tightlist
  \item
    \textbf{==} : eÅŸittir.
  \item
    \textbf{!= } : eÅŸit deÄŸildir.
  \item
    \textbf{\textgreater,\textgreater=,\textless,\textless= } : bÃ¼yÃ¼ktÃ¼r, bÃ¼yÃ¼k eÅŸittir,\ldots.
  \item
    \textbf{\%in\%} : bir ya da birden fazla deÄŸerin varlÄ±ÄŸÄ±nÄ± kontrol eder.
  \end{itemize}
\item
  MantÄ±ksal OperatÃ¶rlerin kombinasyonlarÄ± da kullanÄ±labilir.

  \begin{itemize}
  \tightlist
  \item
    \textbf{\&}: ve
  \item
    \textbf{\textbar{}}: ve ya
  \item
    \textbf{!}: deÄŸil
  \end{itemize}
\item
  PISA verisinde anne eÄŸitim dÃ¼zeyi lisansÃ¼stÃ¼ olan Ã¶ÄŸrencilerin seÃ§ilmesi
\end{itemize}

\hypertarget{summarize-fonksiyonlarux131}{%
\section{summarize() fonksiyonlarÄ±}\label{summarize-fonksiyonlarux131}}

\begin{itemize}
\item
  \textbf{summarize()} seÃ§ilen sÃ¼tunlar iÃ§in her satÄ±rÄ± kullanarak istatistikler hesaplar.
\item
  kaÃ§ satÄ±r olduÄŸu
\item
  ortalamanÄ±n ne olduÄŸu
\item
  toplamÄ±n ne olduÄŸu
\item
  minumum ve maksimum deÄŸerlerin ne olduÄŸu gibi..
\item
  Tek satÄ±rlÄ±k veri setini Ã¶zetleyerek yeni bir veri seti oluÅŸturan fonksiyondur.

  \begin{itemize}
  \tightlist
  \item
    \textbf{min(x)} x vektÃ¶rÃ¼ndeki minumum deÄŸer
  \item
    \textbf{max(x)} x vektÃ¶rÃ¼ndeki maksimum deÄŸer
  \item
    \textbf{mean(x)} x vektÃ¶rÃ¼ndeki ortalama deÄŸer
  \item
    \textbf{median(x)} x vektÃ¶rÃ¼ndeki ortanca deÄŸer
  \item
    \textbf{quantile(x, p)} x vektÃ¶rÃ¼ndeki q. yuzdelik
  \item
    \textbf{sd(x)} x vektÃ¶rÃ¼ndeki standart sapma
  \item
    \textbf{var(x)} x vektÃ¶rÃ¼ndeki varyans
  \item
    \textbf{diff(range(x))} x vektÃ¶rÃ¼ndeki deÄŸiskenlik
  \item
    \textbf{first(x)} x vektÃ¶rÃ¼ndeki ilk eleman
  \item
    \textbf{last(x)} x vektÃ¶rÃ¼ndeki son eleman
  \item
    \textbf{nth(x, n)} x vektÃ¶rÃ¼ndeki n.~eleman
  \item
    \textbf{n()} x vektÃ¶rÃ¼ndeki eleman sayÄ±sÄ±
  \item
    \textbf{n\_distinct(x)} x vektÃ¶rÃ¼ndeki farklÄ± deÄŸerlerin sayÄ±sÄ±
  \end{itemize}
\item
  PISA veri setindeki baÅŸarÄ±sÄ± iÃ§in hesaplanan 10 olasÄ± puan deÄŸerinden (plausible value) ilki kullanÄ±lmÄ±ÅŸtÄ±r.

\begin{itemize}

\item
  \textbf{transmute()} fonksiyonu kullanÄ±larak yeni deÄŸiÅŸken oluÅŸturulduÄŸunda, iÅŸlemde kullanÄ±lan deÄŸiÅŸkenler veri setinden Ã§Ä±karÄ±lÄ±r.
\end{itemize}

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{zevk }\SpecialCharTok{\%\textgreater{}\%}

\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{verbatim}
## # A tibble: 2 x 1
##   toplam
##    <dbl>
## 1      6
## 2     14
\end{verbatim}

\begin{itemize}
\item
  Fonksiyonda Ã¼retilen ilk deÄŸiÅŸken kullanÄ±larak da yeni deÄŸiÅŸken Ã¼retilebilir.
\item
  Ilk olarak Ã¶zyeterliÄŸi Ã¶lÃ§en maddelerden yeni bir veri oluÅŸturulmuÅŸ, daha sonra bu puanlarÄ±n Ã¶nce toplam puanlarÄ± daha sonra toplam puanlarÄ±n kareleri alÄ±nmÄ±ÅŸtÄ±r.
\end{itemize}

\hypertarget{join-fonksiyonu}{%
\section{\texorpdfstring{\textbf{join()} fonksiyonu}{join() fonksiyonu}}\label{join-fonksiyonu}}

\begin{itemize}
\item
  \textbf{join()} fonksiyonlarÄ± iki veri setini istenilen ÅŸekilde birleÅŸtirme amacÄ±yla kullanÄ±lÄ±rlar..
\item
  \textbf{A} ve \textbf{B} veri setlerini birleÅŸtirmek istediÄŸimizde

  \begin{itemize}
  \item
    Her iki veri setinden de hangi \textbf{satÄ±rlarÄ±} almak istiyoruz?
  \item
    Her iki veri setinden de hangi \textbf{sÃ¼tunlarÄ±} almak istiyoruz?
  \item
    SatÄ±rlarÄ±n \textbf{eÅŸleÅŸip eÅŸleÅŸmeyeceÄŸini} hangi deÄŸiÅŸkenlerle belirleyeceÄŸiz?
  \end{itemize}
\end{itemize}

\hypertarget{join-tuxfcrleri}{%
\section{Join TÃ¼rleri}\label{join-tuxfcrleri}}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  Ã‡ok sayÄ±da \textbf{join()} fonksiyonu bulunmaktadÄ±r.
\item
  \textbf{A \%\textgreater\% left\_join(B)}
\end{itemize}

\texttt{A} dan tÃ¼m satÄ±rlarÄ±, mÃ¼mkÃ¼n olduÄŸunda \texttt{B} ile eÅŸleÅŸtir (olmadÄ±ÄŸÄ±nda ``NA'' verir), hem \texttt{A} hem de \texttt{B} den gelen sÃ¼tunlarÄ± alÄ±r.

\begin{center}\includegraphics[width=0.6\linewidth]{images/left_join} \end{center}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  \textbf{A \%\textgreater\% right\_join(B)}
\end{itemize}

\texttt{B} den tÃ¼m satÄ±rlarÄ±, mÃ¼mkÃ¼n olduÄŸunda \texttt{A} ile eÅŸleÅŸtir (olmadÄ±ÄŸÄ±nda ``NA'' verir), hem \texttt{A} hem de \texttt{B} den gelen sÃ¼tunlarÄ± alÄ±r.

\begin{center}\includegraphics[width=0.6\linewidth]{images/right_join} \end{center}

\begin{itemize}
\item
  Pratikte genellike \textbf{left\_join()} kullanÄ±lÄ±r.
\item
  \textbf{A \%\textgreater\% inner\_join(B)}
  yanlÄ±zca \texttt{A} ve \texttt{B} nin eÅŸleÅŸen satÄ±rlarÄ±nÄ± birleÅŸtirir. Hem \texttt{A} hem de \texttt{B} den gelen sÃ¼tunlarÄ± alÄ±r.
\end{itemize}

\begin{center}\includegraphics[width=0.75\linewidth]{images/inner_join} \end{center}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  \textbf{A \%\textgreater\% full\_join(B)}
\end{itemize}

\texttt{A} ve \texttt{B} den tÃ¼m satÄ±rlarÄ± birleÅŸtirir. Hem \texttt{A} hem de \texttt{B} den gelen sÃ¼tunlarÄ± alÄ±r.

\begin{center}\includegraphics[width=0.75\linewidth]{images/full_join} \end{center}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  \textbf{A \%\textgreater\% semi\_join(B)}
\end{itemize}

\texttt{A} nÄ±n \texttt{B} ile eÅŸleÅŸen satÄ±rlarÄ±nÄ± alÄ±r. Sadece \texttt{A} dan gelen sÃ¼tunlarÄ± alÄ±r.

\begin{center}\includegraphics[width=0.75\linewidth]{images/semi_join} \end{center}

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  \textbf{A \%\textgreater\% anti\_join(B)}
  \texttt{A} nÄ±n \texttt{B} ile eÅŸleÅŸemeyen satÄ±rlarÄ±nÄ± alÄ±r. Sadece \texttt{A} dan gelen sÃ¼tunlarÄ± alÄ±r.
\end{itemize}

\begin{center}\includegraphics[width=0.75\linewidth]{images/anti_join} \end{center}

\begin{itemize}
\item
  AynÄ± deÄŸerleri iÃ§eren satÄ±rlarÄ±n olduÄŸu sÃ¼tunlarÄ±n \emph{eÅŸleÅŸmesi} gerektiÄŸini sÃ¶ylÃ¼yoruz.
\item
  BunlarÄ± birleÅŸtirme iÃ§in bir \textbf{by =} argÃ¼manÄ±nÄ± kullanÄ±yoruz.
\item
  EÄŸer birleÅŸtirme yapmak istediÄŸimiz sÃ¼tun/larÄ±n isimleri aynÄ± ise \textbf{by =} argÃ¼manÄ±nÄ± kullanmaya gerek yoktur.
\end{itemize}

\begin{itemize}
\item
  Herhangi bir ek iÅŸlem (yani veri iÅŸleme) yapmadan iÃ§e aktarÄ±lan veri setini kullanarak Ã¶rneklemimizin demografik Ã¶zellikleri hakkÄ±nda bazÄ± temel tanÄ±mlayÄ±cÄ± bilgileri hesaplayabilir ve Ã§izebilirsiniz.   \begin{itemize}
  \item
    Veri kÃ¼mesi PISA\_STU\_2018 ile baÅŸlayÄ±n ve ardÄ±ndan;
  \item
    DeÄŸiÅŸken MISCED (anne eÄŸitim) gÃ¶re gruplayÄ±n ve ardÄ±ndan;

    Her gruptaki gÃ¶zlemlerin sayÄ±sÄ±nÄ± sayÄ±n ve ardÄ±ndan;
  \item
    GruplandÄ±rmayÄ± kaldÄ±rÄ±n
  \end{itemize}
\end{itemize}

## 7      6   887
## 8     NA    55
\end{verbatim}

\begin{itemize}
\item
  \texttt{group\_by()} fonkisyonu veri setinin yÃ¼zey dÃ¼zeyinde deÄŸiÅŸikliklere neden olmaz, bunun yerine temel yapÄ±yÄ± deÄŸiÅŸtirir, bÃ¶ylece gruplar belirtilirse, daha sonra Ã§aÄŸrÄ±lan fonkisyonlar gruplama deÄŸiÅŸkeninin her dÃ¼zeyinde ayrÄ± ayrÄ± gerÃ§ekleÅŸtirilir. \item
  Bu nedenle yukarÄ±daki kod, MISCED deÄŸiÅŸkeninin her bir grubundaki gÃ¶zlem sayÄ±sÄ±nÄ± sayar. EÄŸer sadece toplam gÃ¶zlem sayÄ±sÄ±na ihtiyacÄ±nÄ±z varsa, group\_by() ve ungroup() satÄ±rlarÄ±nÄ± kaldÄ±rabilirsiniz, bÃ¶ylece iÅŸlemi gruplar yerine tÃ¼m veri seti Ã¼zerinde gerÃ§ekleÅŸtirebilirsiniz:
\item
  Benzer ÅŸekilde, Ã¶rneklemin ortalama baÅŸarÄ±sÄ±nÄ± (ve SD'sini) hesaplamak isteyebiliriz ve bunu dplyr/tidyverse paketindeki \texttt{summarise()} fonkisyonu kullanarak yapabiliriz.
\end{itemize}

\begin{itemize}
\item
  Bu kod, baÅŸarÄ± ortalamasÄ±nÄ±n hesaplanmasÄ±nÄ±n sonucunu iÃ§eren ort adlÄ± bir sÃ¼tun biÃ§iminde Ã¶zet veriler Ã¼retir. \item
  YukarÄ±daki kodun bu iÅŸlemin sonucunu kaydetmeyeceÄŸini, sadece konsolda Ã§Ä±ktÄ±sÄ±nÄ± vereceÄŸini unutmayÄ±n. Ä°leride kullanmak Ã¼zere kaydetmek isterseniz, \textless- notasyonunu kullanarak bir nesnede saklayabilir ve daha sonra nesne adÄ±nÄ± yazarak yazdÄ±rabilirsiniz.
\item
  Son olarak, \texttt{group\_by()} fonksiyonu Ã¶zet istatistikleri hesaplarken aynÄ± ÅŸekilde Ã§alÄ±ÅŸacaktÄ±r
\item
  \texttt{group\_by()} fonksiyonundan sonra Ã§aÄŸrÄ±lan iÅŸlevin Ã§Ä±ktÄ±sÄ± gruplama deÄŸiÅŸkeninin her dÃ¼zeyi iÃ§in Ã¼retilecektir.

\begin{itemize}

  AÃ§Ä±lÄ±mÄ± grafiÄŸin grameri (grammer of graphics) ÅŸeklindedir.
\item
  \textbf{lattice} grafiklerindeki gibi grafikler nesneler olarak kaydedilmekte ve birden Ã§ok grafiÄŸi tek bir grafiÄŸin Ã¼zerinde gÃ¶sterebilmektedir.
\item
  \textbf{lattice} paketine gÃ¶re en Ã¶nemli farkÄ± \textbf{katman} mantÄ±ÄŸÄ±yla Ã§alÄ±ÅŸmasÄ±dÄ±r.

  \begin{itemize}
  \tightlist
  \item
    Metin ekleme,
  \item
    renklendirme,
  \item
    aÃ§Ä±klama kutucuklarÄ± vb\ldots{} Ã¶zelleÅŸtirmeler toplama \textbf{(+)} iÅŸareti ile kodlara eklenebilmektedir.
  \end{itemize}
\item
  \textbf{ggplot2} paketnde Temel FonksiyonlarÄ±n KullanÄ±mÄ± aÅŸaÄŸÄ±daki ÅŸekildedir.

\begin{verbatim}
-   **qplot()** ve **ggplot()** fonksiyonlarÄ±
-   **qplot()**, hÄ±zlÄ± grafik (quick plot) Ã§izimi anlamÄ±na gelmektedir.

  -   **qplot(x, y, data, geom)** veya

  -   **ggplot(x, y, data, geom)** veya

  -   **ggplot( data, aes(x, y)) + geom.grafikismi()**
\end{verbatim}
\item
  \textbf{aes()} her bir deÄŸiÅŸkenin alacaÄŸÄ± rolÃ¼ belirlemede kullanÄ±lÄ±r.
\item
  \textbf{geom()} argÃ¼manÄ± Ã§izilecek grafiÄŸi tÃ¼rÃ¼nÃ¼ belirlemek iÃ§in kullanÄ±lmaktadÄ±r. Geometrik nesneler (geometric objects) olarak adlandÄ±rÄ±lmaktadÄ±r.
\item
  Ã–rneÄŸin \textbf{yoÄŸunluk grafiÄŸi} Ã§izilmek istendiÄŸinde;

  \begin{itemize}
  \item
    \textbf{ggplot(x, y, data, geom=``density'')} veya
  \item
    \textbf{ggplot( data, aes(x, y)) + geom.density()}
  \end{itemize}
\item
  ggplot2 paketinde yer alan tÃ¼m grafikler aÅŸaÄŸÄ±da listelenmiÅŸtir.
\end{itemize}

\hypertarget{appendix-appendices}{%
\appendix}


\hypertarget{installing-r}{%
\chapter{\texorpdfstring{Installing \texttt{R}}{Installing R}}\label{installing-r}}

Installing R and RStudio is usually straightforward. The sections below explain how and \href{https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=lVKMsaWju8w}{there is a helpful YouTube video here}.

\hypertarget{installing-base-r}{%
\section{Installing Base R}\label{installing-base-r}}

\href{https://cran.rstudio.com/}{Install base R}. Choose the download link for your operating system (Linux, Mac OS X, or Windows).

If you have a Mac, install the latest release from the newest \texttt{R-x.x.x.pkg} link (or a legacy version if you have an older operating system). After you install R, you should also install \href{http://xquartz.macosforge.org/}{XQuartz} to be able to use some visualisation packages.

If you are installing the Windows version, choose the ``\href{https://cran.rstudio.com/bin/windows/base/}{base}'' subdirectory and click on the download link at the top of the page. After you install R, you should also install \href{https://cran.rstudio.com/bin/windows/Rtools/}{RTools}; use the ``recommended'' version highlighted near the top of the list.

If you are using Linux, choose your specific operating system and follow the installation instructions.

\hypertarget{installing-rstudio}{%
\section{Installing RStudio}\label{installing-rstudio}}

Go to \href{https://www.rstudio.com/products/rstudio/download/\#download}{rstudio.com} and download the RStudio Desktop (Open Source License) version for your operating system under the list titled \textbf{Installers for Supported Platforms}.

\hypertarget{rstudio-settings}{%
\section{RStudio Settings}\label{rstudio-settings}}

There are a few settings you should fix immediately after updating RStudio. Go to \textbf{\texttt{Global\ Options...}} under the \textbf{\texttt{Tools}} menu (âŒ˜,), and in the General tab, uncheck the box that says \textbf{\texttt{Restore\ .RData\ into\ workspace\ at\ startup}}. If you keep things around in your workspace, things will get messy, and unexpected things will happen. You should always start with a clear workspace. This also means that you never want to save your workspace when you exit, so set this to \textbf{\texttt{Never}}. The only thing you want to save are your scripts.

You may also want to change the appearance of your code. Different fonts and themes can sometimes help with visual difficulties or \href{https://datacarpentry.org/blog/2017/09/coding-and-dyslexia}{dyslexia}.

\begin{figure}

{\centering \includegraphics[width=1\linewidth]{images/rstudio_settings_general_appearance} 

}

\caption{RStudio General and Appearance settings}\label{fig:settings-general}
\end{figure}

You may also want to change the settings in the Code tab. Foe example, Lisa prefers two spaces instead of tabs for my code and likes to be able to see the whitespace{} characters. But these are all a matter of personal preference.

\begin{figure}

{\centering \includegraphics[width=1\linewidth]{images/rstudio_settings_code} 

}

\caption{RStudio Code settings}\label{fig:settings-code}
\end{figure}

\hypertarget{installing-latex}{%
\section{Installing LaTeX}\label{installing-latex}}

You can install the LaTeX typesetting system to produce PDF reports from RStudio. Without this additional installation, you will be able to produce reports in HTML but not PDF. This course will not require you to make PDFs. To generate PDF reports, you will additionally need to install tinytex \citep{R-tinytex} and run the following code:

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\NormalTok{tinytex}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{install\_tinytex}\NormalTok{()}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\hypertarget{appendix-updating-r}{%
\chapter{Updating R, RStudio, and packages}\label{appendix-updating-r}}

From time-to-time, updated version of R, RStudio, and the packages you use (e.g., ggplot) will become available. Remember that each of these are separate, so they each have a different process and come with different considerations. We recommend updating to the latest version of all three at the start of each academic year.

\hypertarget{updating-rstudio}{%
\section{Updating RStudio}\label{updating-rstudio}}

RStudio is the easiest component to update. Typically, updates to RStudio won't affect your code, instead they add in new features, like spell-check or upgrades to what RStudio can do. There's usually very little downside to updating RStudio and it's easy to do.

Click \texttt{Help\ -\ Check\ for\ updates}

\begin{figure}

{\centering \includegraphics[width=1\linewidth]{images/update_rstudio} 

}

\caption{Updating RStudio}\label{fig:img-updaterstudio}
\end{figure}

If an update is available, it will prompt you to download it and you can install it as usual.

\hypertarget{updating-r}{%
\section{Updating R}\label{updating-r}}

Finally, you may also wish to update R itself. The key thing to be aware of is that when you update R, if you just download the latest version from the website, you will lose all your packages.

\hypertarget{windows}{%
\subsection{Windows}\label{windows}}

The easiest way to update R on Windows and not cause yourself a huge headache is to use the \texttt{installr} package. When you use the \texttt{updateR()} function, a series of dialogue boxes will appear. These should be fairly self-explanatory but there is a \href{https://www.r-statistics.com/2015/06/a-step-by-step-screenshots-tutorial-for-upgrading-r-on-windows/}{full step-by-step guide available} for how to use \texttt{installr}, the important bit is to select ``Yes'' when it asked if you would like to copy your packages from the older version of R.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Install the installr package}
\FunctionTok{install.packages}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"installr"}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Run the update function}
\NormalTok{installR}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{updateR}\NormalTok{()}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\hypertarget{mac}{%
\subsection{Mac}\label{mac}}

For a Mac, you can use the updateR package. You'll need to install this from GitHub. You will be asked to type your system password (that you use to log into your computer) in the console pane. If relevant, it will ask you if you want to restore your packages for a new major version.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# install from github}
\NormalTok{devtools}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{install\_github}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"AndreaCirilloAC/updateR"}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# update your R version, you will need your system password}
\NormalTok{updateR}\SpecialCharTok{::}\FunctionTok{updateR}\NormalTok{()}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\hypertarget{updating-packages}{%
\section{Updating packages}\label{updating-packages}}

Package developers will occasionally release updates to their packages. This is typically to add in new functions to the package, or to fix or amend existing functions. \textbf{Be aware that some package updates may cause your previous code to stop working}. This does not tend to happen with minor updates to packages, but occasionally with major updates, you can have serious issues if the developer has made fundamental changes to how the code works. For this reason, we recommend updating all your packages once at the beginning of each academic year (or semester) - don't do it before an assessment or deadline just in case!

To update an individual package, the easiest way is to use the \texttt{install.packages()} function, as this always installs the most recent version of the package.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\FunctionTok{install.packages}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"tidyverse"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

To update multiple packages, or indeed all packages, RStudio provides helpful tools. Click \texttt{Tools\ -\ Check\ for\ Package\ Updates}. A dialogue box will appear and you can select the packages you wish to update. Be aware that if you select all packages, this may take some time and you will be unable to use R whilst the process completes.

\begin{figure}

{\centering \includegraphics[width=1\linewidth]{images/update_packages} 

}

\caption{Updating packages with RStudio}\label{fig:img-updateall}
\end{figure}

\hypertarget{package-install-troubleshooting}{%
\section{Troubleshooting}\label{package-install-troubleshooting}}

Occasionally, you might have a few problem packages that seemingly refuse to update. For me, \texttt{rlang} and \texttt{vctrs} cause me no end of trouble. These aren't packages that you will likely every explicitly load, but they're required beneath the surface for R to do things like knit your Markdown files etc.

\hypertarget{non-zero-exit-status}{%
\subsection{Non-zero exit status}\label{non-zero-exit-status}}

If you try to update a package and get an error message that says something like \texttt{Warning\ in\ install.packages\ :\ installation\ of\ package\ â€˜vctrsâ€™\ had\ non-zero\ exit\ status} or perhaps \texttt{Error\ in\ loadNamespace(i,\ c(lib.loc,\ .libPaths()),\ versionCheck\ =\ vI{[}{[}i{]}{]})\ :\ \ namespace\ \textquotesingle{}rlang\textquotesingle{}\ 0.4.9\ is\ being\ loaded,\ but\ \textgreater{}=\ 0.4.10\ is\ required} one solution I have found is to manually uninstall the package, restart R, and then install the package new, rather than trying to update an existing version. The \texttt{installr} package also has a useful function for uninstalling packages.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# Load installr}
\FunctionTok{library}\NormalTok{(installr)}

\CommentTok{\# Uninstall the problem package}
\FunctionTok{uninstall.packages}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"package\_name"}\NormalTok{)}

\CommentTok{\# Then restart R using session {-} restart R}
\CommentTok{\# Then install the package fresh}

\FunctionTok{install.packages}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"package"}\NormalTok{)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\hypertarget{cannot-open-file}{%
\subsection{Cannot open file}\label{cannot-open-file}}

You may get the following error after trying to install any packages at all:

\begin{quote}
Error in install packages : Cannot open file `C:/\ldots..': Permission denied
\end{quote}

This usually indicates a permissions problem with writing to the default library (the folder that packages are kept in). Sometimes this means that you need to install R and RStudio as administrator or run it as administrator.

One other fix may be to change the library location using the following code (check in ``C:/Program Files/R'' for what version you should have instead of ``R-3.5.2''):

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# change the library path}
\FunctionTok{.libPaths}\NormalTok{(}\FunctionTok{c}\NormalTok{(}\StringTok{"C:/Program Files/R/R{-}3.5.2/library"}\NormalTok{))}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

If that works and you can install packages, set this library path permanently:

\begin{enumerate}
\def\labelenumi{\arabic{enumi}.}
\tightlist
\item
  Install the usethis package
\item
  Run \texttt{usethis::edit\_r\_profile()} in the console; it will open up a blank file
\item
  Paste into the file (your version of): \texttt{.libPaths(c("C:/Program\ Files/R/R-3.5.2/library"))}
\item
  Save and close the file
\item
  Restart R for changes to take effect
\end{enumerate}

The code in your .Rprofile will now run every time you start up R.

As always, if you're having issues, please ask on Teams or come to office hours.

\hypertarget{conventions}{%
\chapter{Conventions}\label{conventions}}

This book will use the following conventions:

\begin{itemize}
\tightlist
\item
  Generic code: \texttt{list(number\ =\ 1,\ letter\ =\ "A")}
\item
  Highlighted code: {{dplyr}{::}{slice\_max}{(}{)}}
\item
  File paths: data/sales.csv
\item

  What is a p-value?
\item
  \begin{enumerate}
  \def\labelenumi{(\Alph{enumi})}
  \tightlist
  \item
    the probability that the null hypothesis is true\\
  \end{enumerate}
\item
  \begin{enumerate}
  \def\labelenumi{(\Alph{enumi})}
  \setcounter{enumi}{1}
  \tightlist
  \item
    the probability of the observed (or more extreme) data, under the assumption that the null-hypothesis is true\\
  \end{enumerate}

  \def\labelenumi{(\Alph{enumi})}
  \setcounter{enumi}{2}
  \tightlist
  \item
    the probability of making an error in your conclusion
  \end{enumerate}

\hypertarget{glossary-1}{%
\chapter{Glossary}\label{glossary-1}}

You can use the \texttt{glossary()} function to automatically link to a term in the \href{https://psyteachr.github.io/glossary/}{psyTeachR glossary} or make your own project-specific glossary.

This will create a link to the glossary and include a tooltip with a short definition when you hover over the term. Use the following syntax in inline r: \texttt{glossary("word")}. For example, common data types{} are integer{}, double{}, and character{}.

If you need to link to a definition, but are using a different form of the word, add the display version as the second argument (\texttt{display}). You can also override the automatic short definition by providing your own in the third argument (\texttt{def}). Add the argument \texttt{link\ =\ FALSE} if you just want the hover definition and not a link to the psyTeachR glossary.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\CommentTok{\# glossary("data type", }
\CommentTok{\#          display = "Data Types", }
\CommentTok{\#          def = "My custom definition of data types", }
\CommentTok{\#          link = FALSE)}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

You can add a glossary table to the end of a chapter with the following code. It creates a table of all terms used in that chapter previous to the \texttt{glossary\_table()} function. It uses \texttt{kableExtra()}, so if you use it in a code chunk, set \texttt{results=\textquotesingle{}asis\textquotesingle{}}.

\begin{Shaded}
\begin{Highlighting}[]
\FunctionTok{glossary\_table}\NormalTok{()}
\end{Highlighting}
\end{Shaded}

\begin{table}
\centering
\begin{tabular}{l|l}
\hline
term & definition\\
\hline
character & \\
\hline
data type & \\
\hline
double & \\
\hline
integer & \\
\hline
\end{tabular}
\end{table}

If you want to contribute to the glossary, fork the \href{https://github.com/PsyTeachR/glossary}{github project}, add your terms and submit a pull request, or suggest a new term at the \href{https://github.com/PsyTeachR/glossary/issues}{issues page}.
